comytted leue goddes iudgemet none euell capitayn warre whiche disposicion enclyned peace sodry victory ouerthrowes neuer defaute owne person either lacke hardynes polytike order fre dispences somwhat aboue power lyberall wt large giftes gatte hym vnstedfast fredship whiche cause fayn borowe pil extorte place gat hym stedfast hatred close secrete depe dyssymuler lowly coutenauce arrogate herte outwardly famylyer inwardly hated lettyng kysse whome thought kyll dispiteous cruell alwaye eiuyll wyll ambycion serue purpose frende fooe wer indifferent auau tage grewe spared mane death whose lyfe withstode purpose slewe towre kyng henry vi saiyng nowe heyre male kyng edward thyrde house yorke whiche murder done without kynge edwardes assent whiche would haue appoynted bocherlye office rather owne brother wise also wene yt hys drift lacked helpyng forth owne brother clarence death whiche thyng apparaunce resisted although inwardly mynded cause thereof men notynge doynges procedynges marke longe kyng edwardes tyme thought opteyne croune case kyng brother whose life loked euyl dyet would sone shorten happe disease dede chyldre beyng youg yt duke clarence lyued pretensed purpose farre hyndered yf duke clarence kept hym self true nephewe yong kyng would haue take vpo kyng euery one caste troumpe duke gloucester waye sure hys brother clarence dead knewe might woorke without ieopardye poyntes certentie whosoeuer deuyneth coiectureth maye well shote ferre shorte coiecture afterward toke place fewe dooe shall ceaue afore declare howe rychard duke gloucestre began mischeuous imagened pretenced enterprise apantly shalbe opened must litle putte remebrauce louyng charitable acte lesse profitable amiable yt whole comynaltie inwardely thought outwardly dissimuled whiche kyng edward liyng deathe bedde long dyed life althoughe deuision emongest frendes somewhat greued yrked hym yet helth lesse regarded tooke hede reason yt thought yt hable thynges rule bothe tie thei neuer obstinate last sickenesse whiche cotinued longer false fantasticall tale haue vntruly falsely surmised self wrote pamphlet truly knew whe perceiued natural stregth gone hoped litle recouery artes al phicysyans whiche perceaued onely prolong life began consider youth child howe nothyng lesse mistrusted happened yet wisely forseyng consideryng many harmes might ensue yt debate noble ye youth child lacke discrecion good counsaill frendes knew well euery part would woorke owne comoditee rather plesaunt aduise wynne theim selfes fauour fitable aduertismet yt childre good wherfore liyng death bed westminster called hym suche lordes wer aboute hym knewe variaunce especiall lord marque dorset soonne quene lord hastynges ye quene especially grudged yt fauor yt kyng bare hym also thought familier wt kyng waton copaignie hir kynne bare hym sore aswel yt ye kyng made hym capitain caleys office ye lord riuers brother ye quene claimed yt kynges former promise diuerse giftes whiche receaued yt thei loked lordes wt diuerse party come vnto yt kynges presens caused hymself raised vp wt pillous ca gesse saied exhortacyo kynge edward thus muche like setece theim lordes dere kynsme alies plight nowe lye se fectly fele yt whiche looke yt lesse liue wt therfore yt depely moued care case leue suche leue suche child like fynd whiche thei shuld fynd variauce god forbid thei theim felfes might hap fall werre discresio wuld serue set peace youth whiche reke onely suerty rest concord suffiseth loue theim eche hate thei wer feithfullnes might hap suffice childhod must mainteined menes autorite slip youth vnderpropted wt elder cousaill whiche thei neuer haue except geue geue except agre wher eche laboureth breake maketh hatred eche impugneth others cousail ther must nedes log tract good coclusio forward ferther eche tie laboreth chief flaterer adulacio shall haue place plain feithful aduise whiche must nedes ensue yt euill bringyng vp price whose mynd teder youth infecte shall redily fall mischief riot drawe doune noble realme ruyne grace turne hym wisdome whiche god sed hym thei eiuill meanes pleased hym best shall fal farthest fauour yt ye legth euell driftes driue naught good plain wayes sper florishe great variauce hath euer bee betwene alwais great cause tyme thyng right wel entedid miscostrued hath turned yt woorse smal displeasure dooe ether owne affecio ether instigacio eiuill tooges hath sore agrauate wot well neuer great cause hatred haue loue men yt christe leaue prechers tell yet wot whether pchers wordes ought moue yt gooyng place yt thei preche shal desire remebre yt one part beyng blod yt alies eche wt either kynred affinite whiche yt spirituall affinitie kynred christ taker yt sacamentes christes churche weight whiche cosanguynite beare would god moued spirituall charite fleshly cosanguinyte lord forbid yt loue yt woorse together self cause yt ought loue better yet yt ofte happeneth wher fynd dedly emogest theim whiche nature lawe moost ought agre together suche serpent ambicio desire vanyne glory souere ingtie whiche emogest estate entered crepith foorth ferre till wt deuision varyaunce turneth mischief first longyng bee next yt best afterward egall wt beest last chief aboue yt beest whiche immoderate appetite woorship debate discencion yt grewe losse sorowe trouble hath win fewe yeres growen realme praye god well forget well remebre whiche thyng could aswell haue forsene haue wt pane pleasure proued god de blessed lady yt commo othe would neuer haue wonne curtesyes mennes knee losse many heddes sith thynges passed called agayn muche ought bee ware occasion haue taken great hurte eftsones fall yt occasion nowe bee greues passed quiet thanked bee god likely well prosper welthfull peace vnder cousin child god send theim life loue co cord whiche ii thynges yt lesse losse wer thei though god pleasure yet realme alwayes fynd kynges aduetur good kynges thei emogest selfes childes reigne fall debate many good manne shall innocently perishe happely also long fynd peace quiet wherfore last woordes yt euer looke speake exhort require loue haue borne yt loue haue borne loue yt lord bereth v fro tyme forward greues forgotte eche loue verely trust wyll yf thyng regarde god kynges affinitee kynred realme owne cou tre owne suretie wealthe al kyng fayntnes longer endurynge syt vp layde hym downe right side face toward theim ther none presente yt could forbeare wepyng yt lordes cofortynge hym wt good woordes thei could answeryng yt tyme thought stande pleasure presence theyr wordes appeared eche forgaue ioyned theyr ha de together appeared theyr dedes harte farre asoder fewe dayes thys noble prynce dysceased westmynster ix daye apryll yere lorde cccc lxxxiii reygned xxii yeres one moneth viii dayes wt great funeral pompe conueyed wyndsore leuyng behynd hym ii soonnes edwarde prynce story entreateth chylde xiii yeres age richarde duke yorke ii yeres yonger prince fiue doughters elizabeth goddes grace maryed kyng henry vii mother kyng hery ye eyght cycile fortunate fayre fyrst wedded ye vycout welles one kyne lyued great wealth brydget professed selfe close nonne syon anne maryed lorde thomas hauwarde erle surrey duke norffolke katheryne yt yogest doughter maryed lorde willya courtney sonne yt earle deuoshire logtyme tossed fortune somtyme welth aduersitee tyl yt benignitee nephewe kyng herye ye viii brought sure estate accordyng degre geny kyng edward suche prince gouernaunce behaueour tyme peace desc ipcio edward fourth tyme warre eche must others enemye yt ther neuer kyng realme attaynyng croune warre battayle hartely beloued substaunce people hym selfe specially fauoured parte life yt tyme death whiche fauoure affeccion yet death crueltie myschiefe trouble tempesteous world folowed highlye towardes hym encreased suche time died displeasure bare hym grudge kyng henry yt vi sake deposed wel assuaged effect quenched within yt space xxii yeres great part man life wer reconsiled growen fauour neuer strauge true harte demaunded goodly personage princely beholde hert couragious politike councell aduersitee nothyng abashed prosperitee rather ioyful proude peace iuste mercyfull warre sharpe fearce felde bold hardie yet neuer thelesse farther reason policie woulde aduenture whose warres whosoeuer circumspectly aduisedly considereth shal lesse comend wisdome policie auoyded theim manhode vanquished theim visage full faced louelie bodie mightie stronge cleane made ouer lyberall wato dyet waxed somewhat corpulet bourly neuerthelesse vncomely youth greatly geuen fleshely wantones yt health bodie great prosperitee fortune especiall grace hardlye refrayneth thys faulte litle greued people neyther coulde one mannes pleasure stretche extende displeasure veraye many multitude bee greued priuate mannes fantesie volupteousnesse whe doe wtout violece latter dayes left al wild daliauce fel grauitee yt brought realme wealthie sperous estate al feare outwarde enemy clerely extinguished warre hande none toward suche looked people wer toward prince costrayned feare true louyng wylfull obedience emongest theimselfe ye common wer good peace lordes whome knewe variaunce death bed thought brought good concord loue amytee lytle death left gatheryng mony subiectes whiche thyng draweth yt heartes englyshme fro kynges prynces nothyng ether entreprysed ndr toke yt shuld dryue thereunto tribute frauce litle recouered obteyned yt yere dyed recouered toune berwike yt kyng scottes albeit yt yt tyme reigne benigne courteous famylyer parte vertues estemed high humilitees yet condycion thende last dayes decayed whiche many prince longe cotinued souereingtie declyne proude porte behaueoure theyr condicions accustomed begynnyng yet lowlynes gentlenes farre forth hym encreased somer died beyng haueryng bowre sente mayre aldermenne london thyther hunte make pastyme made theim hartie famylyer frendlye chere sent also theyr wyues suche plentie venyson one thyng many dayes gatte hym eyther mo heartes hartie fauoure emongest commen people whiche often tymes esteme take greate kyndnes lytle courtesye greate profyte benefyte noble prynce deceassed haue hearde tyme lyfe mooste desyred whe people moste desyred kepe hym whiche loue people entiere affeccio towarde hym bene noble chyldren hauyng theim selfes also many gyftes nature many princely vertues much good towardnesse age coulde receaue meruelous fortresse sure armoure yf deuysion dissencion frendes vnarmed left destitute execrable desyre souereingtie uoked destruccio either kynd kyndnesse holde place muste nedes haue bee chiese defence richarde duke glouceter nature vncle office protectoure father greatly beholden theim othe allegeaunce bounden bandes broken violated bynde manne manne together withoute anye respecte god worlde vnnaturally contryued bereaue theim onely dignytee preheminence also natural lyues worldely felicytee fyrste shewe coniecture pretended thing brother lyfe ye shall vnderstande trueth nyght king edward died one called mistelbrooke long ere daye sprange came house one potier dwelling redcrosse strete withoute creple gate london hastie rapping quickely let saied mistelbrooke shewed vnto potier kyng edward yt nighte deceased trueth potier wil master duke gloucetre kyng warrat cause thinke harde say whether seruaut knewe thing prepensed otherwise inklingther likelihode spake naughte nowe retourne trewe history wer duke gloucetre olde sore practised conclusyon tyme moued therunto put hope tender age young prince nephewes oportunitee likely spede putteth manne courage neuer entended certen northe partyes good gouernaunce countrey aduertised brother deathe contriued destruccion nephewes yt vsurpacion roiall dignitee croune asmuche well wyste holpe maynteine long continued grudge harte burnynge betwene quenes kynred kynges bloodde either parte enuiyng others authorytee nowe thought dede fertherly beginning pursute entent sure grounde situacion vnnaturall building might vnder pretence remebring olde dyspleasures abuse ignoraunce angre one partie destruccion yt wynne purpose many coulde suche coulde bee wonne might bee loste looked therfore one thing certaine intent wer perceaued haue made peace betwene party owne bloodde intente kept secrete tyll knewe frendes ye whiche henry duke buckingham fyrste yt sent hym brother deathe trusty seruaunt called persall cytee yorke duke gloucetre kepte kyng brother funeralles persall came iohn ward secrete chaumberer duke gloucetre desiryng close couerte manier might speake duke maister wherupo deed nyght duke sente persall beyng aduoyded whiche shewed duke gloucetre duke buckingham maister newe worlde would take suche parte woulde woulde farther wayte vpon hym good fellowes yf nede duke sent backe yt messanger great thankes diuerse preuey instruccions mouthe persall somuche trauaile came duke buckyngham maister march wale eftsones newe instruccions met duke gloucetre notingham whiche come oute northcoutrey many knightes gentylmenne noumbre vi c horse iourney towarde london secrete meting comunicacion betwene hym duke gloucetre retourned suche spede yt brought duke buckingham master mete wt duke gloucetre farre northampton iii c horsses twoo came together northampton fyrst beganne vnhappy enterprice duke buckingham contynued stil wt duke gloucetre till crouned kyng ye shall plainly perceaue hereafter younge kyng deathe father kepte housholde ludlowe father sente hym thyther iustice bee doone march wale ende authoritee presence wylde welshemenne euell dysposed personnes shoulde refraine frome accustomed murthers outerages gouernaunce younge prynce comitted lorde anthony wooduile earle riuers lorde scale brother quene wise hardye honourable personage valyaunte hande pollitick counsell assocyate partye effecte euery one nere kinne vnto quene planted nexte aboute prynce dryfte quene semed bee deuysed whereby bloodde myghte ryghte tender youth bee planted prynces fauoure afterwarde shoulde hardely bee eradicated oute duke gloucetre turned distruccion vpon grounde sette foundacion vnhappy building whome soeuer perceaued bee varyaunce theim beare toward hym self fauoure brake vnto theim mouthe writing secrete messenger neither reason yet bee suffered younge kyng maister kinsmanne bee handes custody mother kinrede sequestred maner frome company attendaunce euery one ought hym faithfull seruice many theim farre honorable parte kynne mother syde whose bloodde duke gloucetre sauyng kynges pleasure farre vnmete bee matched whiche nowe bee remoued frome kyng least noble bee lefte aboute hym neyther honourable maiestie v also hym lesse suretye haue noblest mightiest frendes frome hym v lytle ieopardye suffer specially oure well proued euel willers growe greate authorytee wt king youth namely whiche light belefe soone perswaded ye remembre kyng edward hym self albeit age discrecion yet ruled many thinges yt bende stoode either wt honoure oure profyte wyth commoditee anye manne elles excepte onely immoderate aduau cemente theim selues whiche whether thristed sore theyr owne wele harde thynke gesse yf folkes frendshype holden better place wyth kynge anye respecte kynred myghte paraduenture easely haue trapped brought confusyon v thys easly haue done thys nere blood royall oure lorde hathe wroughte hys wyll thanked hys grace perell past beit greate growing suffer young kynge enemyes handes whyche wythoute wyttinge myghte abuse name hys commaundemente af vndoing thynges god good prouysion forbyd whych good prouysion none v hathe thynge lesse nede late attonemente made kynges pleasure place party heartes willes none v vnwise ouersone truste newe frende made olde fooe thynke anye onely kyndenes sodenly contracted houre contynued scantlye yet fortnyght shoulde deper set stomackes longe accustomed malice many yeres rooted perswasions wrytinges yt duke glouceter set fyre theim whiche wer easye kindle especyall twayne henry duke buckyngham wyllyam lorde hastynges lorde chamberlayn menne honour great power one log sucecessio aunceters hys offyces kynges fauoure two bearynge eache muche loue hatred quenes bloodde accorded together duke glouceter would remoue frome kyng mother fredes vnder name theyr enemyes wherupon duke glouceter beynge aduertysed lordes kyng entended brynge london hys coronation acco panyed wyth nomber theyr frendes shoulde harde hym bryng hys purpose passe wythoute assemblinge gathering people maner open warre wherof ende wyst doubtefull whyche kynge beynge syde shoulde haue name face rebellion secretelye therefore dyuers meanes caused quene perswaded nether nede shoulde also bee ieopardeous kinge come vp stronge nowe euery lorde loued none thynge studyed tryumphe coronation honoure yt kyng lordes aboute kyng asseble kinges name much people shuld geue lordes betwyxte whome theim bene tyme debate feare suspecte leaste shoulde gather thys people kynges sauegarde man impugned theyr destruccyon hauynge regarde theyr olde varyaunce theyr newe attonemente whyche cause part myght assemble men also theyr defence whose powres wyste well farre stretched thus al realme fall roare mischiefe thereof shoulde ensue whiche lykly lytle harme lyke fal leaste woulde worlde woulde put kynred blame saiynge vnwselye vntruely broken amytie peace whyche kynge husbande prudently made betwene kinred hys whyche amytee hys kinne alwaies obserued quene beyng thus perswaded sente worde kynge brother cause ner nede assemble anye people also duke glouceter lordes bed wrot vnto kinge reuerently quenes frendes louyngely nothing earthlye mystrustyng broughte young kyng toward london wt sober compaignie greate hast good spede til came northapton fro thece remoued stony stratford whyche daye two duke theyr bende came northampton faynynge stonye stratforde coulde lodge theim founde earle ryuers entendynge nexte moruynge haue folowed kynge bee wyth hym earely mornyng nyght duke made earle riuers frendly chere assone departed verye famylier wyth greate curtesie ope syghte erle riuers lodged ii duke theyr pryuye frendes fell councell wherein spente greate part nyght dawning daye sente pryuely ther seruauntes theyr lodgynges haste horsebacke theyr lordes maner redy ryde wheruppon theyr seruauntes ready lorde ryuers seruauntes wer awake nowe duke taken keyes ynne theyr possession none shoulde yssue oute wythout concente ouer thys hygh way toward stony stratforde set certaine theyr folkes shoulde cause compell retourne person passinge frome northampton stony stratforde sayinge duke theim selfes woulde fyrst come kynge northampton thus bare folkes hande earle ryuers vnderstode gate closed wayes euery syde beset nether hys seruauntes nether hym self suffered goo oute perceauinge great thing wythoute knowledge begon noughte comparyng thys preasent dooynge wyth laste nyghtes cherein fewe houres great chauce marueleously myslyked howbeit syth could get awaye determined kepe self close leaste shoulde seme hyde hym selfe secret fear hys owne faute wherof saw cause selfe wherfore suretie hys owne consience determyned go inquire thys matter myghte meane whome assone saw beganne quarell wyth hym affyrmyng pretended set dystaunce betwene kyng theim bryng theim confucyon whyche lye powre began el oequet manne godly wise excuse hym self thei would aunswer tooke hym force putte hym ward mounted horsback came stony stratford wher kyng goyng horsbacke would leaue lodgyng theim strayte bothe compaignies thei came presence thei alighted compaignie aboute theim knee saluted hym theim getely receaued nothyng erthely knowyng ner mistrustyng yet duke buckyngham saied aloude afore gentlemenne yomenne kepe roumes therwith yt kyng presence thei picked quarell lord rychard grey quenes soonne brother lord marque halfe brother kyng saiyng marque brother lorde ryuers vncle copassed rule kyng realme sette varyauce betwene thestates subdewe destroye noble bloodde realme toward thaccomplishment thesame thei saied lord marque entred toure london thence take oute treasure sent mene sea whiche thynges duke knewe well dooen good purpose necessary appoincted yt whole counsail londo somewhat thei must haue saied vnto whiche woordes kyng aunswered brother marque hath dooen cannot saie good faith dare well aunswer myne vncle ryuers brother thei bee innocent suche mattiers yee leege duke buckyngham thei haue kepte ye dealyng matter farre knowledge good grace foorthwith thei arrested lord rychard sir thomas vaugham sir rychard hawte kyng presence brought kyng northapton thei tooke ferther counsaill affaire thei sent kyng pleased theim set aboute hym suche seruauntes better pleased theim hym whiche dealyng wept booted dynner duke gloucester sent dyshe owne table lorde ryuers praiyng hym bee good chere bee well thanked hym prayed messenger beare nephiewe lord rychard like woordes knewe haue neede conforte one suche aduersite straunge hym self dayes ennured therwith therfore could beare message duke gloucester sent lord ryuers ye lord rychard sir thomas vaughm sir rychard hawte northparties dyuers prisones last came poumfrette thei foure behedded without iudge et maner haue heard duke gloucester tooke hym gouernaunce younge kyng muche reuerence conueighed towardes london tidynges came hastely quene mydnight sore reporte kyng hir soonne taken brother soonne hir frendes arested sent manne wyst whither heuye tydynges quene bewayled childes ruyn hir frendes mischaunce awne infortune curssyng tyme euer perswaded leaue gatheryng people bryng vp kyng greate powre passed therfore nowe tooke hir younger soonne duke yorke hir doughters went oute palais westminster sanctuary lodged abbotes place child compaignie regystred sanctuary persones night came docter rotheram archebysshop yorke lorde chauceloure messenger lorde chambrelayne yorke place besyde westminster messenger brought bysshoppes bed syde declared hym yt duke gone backe younge kyng northampto declared ferther lorde hastynges master sent hym woord feare nothyng bee well well bisshop bee well neuer bee well haue seen messenger depar ted whereupon bysshop called vp seruauntes daye light tooke hym greate seale came daye quene founde muche heuynesse rumble haste busynesse conuerghaunce caryage hir stuffe sanctuary euery manne busye carye beare conueigh stuffe chestes ferdelles manne vnoccupied caryed thei commaunded another place quene sat alone belowe russhes desolate dysmaied archebisshop conforted best maner coulde shewynge matter nothynge sore tooke put good hope oute feare message sente hym fro lorde hastinges wo worth quene goeth aboute destroye bloodde madame good comforte assure yf crowne anye king soonne whome nowe haue shal morowe croune brother haue greate seale lykewise noble husbande delyuered deliuer vse sone therewyth delyuered greate seale departed home dawnynge daye opened windowes looked themys myghte see riuer ful boates duke glouceter hys seruauntes watchyng person shoulde goo sanctuary ner none shoulde passe vnserched great rumoure commocion citee place people diuersly deuined vpo thys dealyng dyuerse lordes knyghtes gentylmen ether fauour quene feare selues assembled compaignies together went flockyng together harneyes many also recompted thys demeanour attempted especyallye agaynst lordes agaynst kyng self dysturbaunce hys coronat ion therefore assembled together common thys matter london archebyshoppe yorke fearynge woulde ascrybed dede ouermuche lightnes sodeynly yelded vp great seale quene whome custodie therof nothyng apperteigned without especiall commaundement yt kyng secretly sent seale agayn brought wyth hym accustomed maner mete lordes metyng lord hastynges whose truthe towarde kyng manne doubted neded doubte perswaded lordes beleue duke glouceter faythfull sure towardes prince yt lord ryuers lorde richard knyghtes apprehended wer matter attempted theim agaynste duke gloucetre buckyngham put vnder arest suretie kynges icopardye also sauegarde remayne tyll matter duke also lordes kynges councell indifferentlye examyned discrecions ordred eyther iudged appesed one thyng aduysed theim beware iudged matter farreforth knewe truthe turnyng theyr pryuate grudge commen hurte irrityng prouokyng men vnto angre disturbyng kynges coronacion toward whiche duke wer co myng might paraduenture bryng yt matter farre ioynte shoulde neuer bee brought frame agayne whiche yf happe lykely come felde though party thynges eguall yet shoulde autoryte bee syde kynge hym selfe persuasyons lorde hastynges whereof parte hym selfe belcued parte wyste well contrarye commocyons somewhat appeased especiall duke buckyngham glouceter wer nere came shortly kynge none maner none voyce sembleaunce coronacion causyng fame blowen suche persones apprehended contryued distruccion duke gloucetre buekyngham noble bloodde thys realme thentent thei alone would rule gouerne kyng coloure therof duke seruauntes rode carte stuffe wer taken amonge stuffe maruayle thoughe harneyes whiche brekynge vp suche housholde muste brought awaye caste awaye shewed people went sayde lo barrelles harneyes traytoures hadde preuely conueighed caryages destroye noble lordes withall dyuerse although made matter wise menne vnlykely well perceauyng thentendoures suche purpose woulde rather haue theyr harnesse theyr backes haue bounde theim vp barrelles yet muche parte commen people therewith ryght well satisfyed kyng approched nere cytie edmonde shawe goldesmythe mayre cytie aldremenne shreues skarlet fyue hundreth commoner murraye receaued grace reuerently harnesaye parke conueighed hym cytee entred fourthe daye maye fyrste laste yeare reigne lodged bisshoppes palayce duke goucetre bare hym open sight reuerently saiyng men rode beholde youre prynce souereygne lorde made suche sembleaunce lowlynes prince frome greate obloquy late sodeynly fallen greate truste councell next assembled made onlye chiefe ruler thoughte mooste mete bee protectoure kynge realme desteny folye lambe betaken wolfe kepe whiche councell archebyshoppe yorke sore blamed delyueryng greate seale quene seale taken hym delyueto docter iohn russell byshoppe lyncolne wyse manne good muche experyence dyuerse lordes knightes appoynted dyuerse roumes lorde chamberlayn kepte roumes yt many nowe protectour whiche alwayes muste take duke gloucetre sore thristed acheuyng pretensed entrepryse thought euerye daye yere tyll perfourmed yet durste ferther attempte aslong hadde halfe praye hys hande well wyttynge yf deposed one brother realme would fall yf remayned sanctuary happely shortelie coueyghed farther libertee wherfore continet next metyng lordes councell purposed theim heynous thyng quene procedyng great lyce toward kynges councelers yt shoulde kepe kynges brother sanctuarye hym whose special pleasure conforte wer haue brother wt hym done none intet bryng ye lordes obloquy murmoure people though wer trusted wt kynges brother lordes wer yt whole as noble yt realme appoynted yt kynges nere frendes ye tuycion royall person prosperitee wherof standeth alonely fro kepyng enemyes euill dyate partely also recreacion moderate pleasure whiche cannot take tendre youth copany old auncient person famylyer conuersacion farre vnder farre aboue age neuerthelesse estate coueniet accompany maiestie wherfore wt rather owne brothere man thinke cosyderacio light thynke man thinketh loueth ye kyng let hym cosyder yt sometyme wt smal thynges greater cannot stande verelye redoundeth greatly ye dyshonoure kynges highnes v bee grace haue come mannes mouthe realme onely also landes euell woordes walke farre yt kynges brother fayne kepe sactuary euery wyl iudge man wil nought opinios fastened mennes hertes harde wrested oute many growe grefe manne diuine wherfore thinketh worste sende quene honourable trustye personage suche tendereth kynges weale honoure counsell also credite fauoure whiche consideracions none semeth meately reuerende father lorde cardinall archbishop cauntourbury maye matter doo mooste good menne yf please hym take paine whiche doubte goodnesse wil refuse kynges sake oures wealth younge duke hym selfe kyn ge moost honorable brother comforte souereigne lord hym selfe moost derest nephiewe considering therby shalbe ceassed sclaunderous rumour obloquy nowe goyng abroade hurtes auoyded yt therof myght ensue must reste quietnesse growe realme percase bee obstinate precisely sette owne wyll opynion neither wyse feithfull aduertysement moue mannes reason satisfye shal myne aduice kynges authoritee fetche hym oute prysone bring hym noble presence whose continuall companye shalbe well cheryshed honorablye intreated worlde shall oure bonoure reproche perceaue onely malyce frowardnesse foly causeth kepe hym minde tyme excepte lordes anye thinge per ceaue contrarye neuer shall goddes grace wedde selfe vnto myne owne wyll shalbe redye chaunge vpon youre better aduice protectoure saied coun cell affirmed mocion good reasonable kyng duke brother honorable thing shoulde ceasse great murmoure realme yf mother myght good meanes bee induced deliuer hym whiche thing archbishop cauntourburye whome agreed also bee moost conuenient thervnto tooke vpon hym moue therto dooe vttermoste endeuoure yf coulde wise bee intreated good wil delyuer hym thought suche spirytualtye presente anye wyse bee attempted take hym oute agaynste wyll woulde bee thyng turne grudge menne high displeasure god pryuiledge place bee broken many yeres kepte whiche bothe kynges bishoppes graunted confyrmed whiche grounde sanctifyed sainct peter hym selfe v hundreth yeres agone syth tyme neuer vndeuoute kynge euer enterprysed sacred priuyledge vyolate holy bishoppe durste presume churche consecrate therfore archbysshoppe god forbyd manne shoulde erthely enterpryse breake immunyte libertee sacred sanctuary hath bene sauegard many good mannes lyfe truste shall nede maner nede would doo trust reason shalbe contented thyng good maner obteigned yf hap bring passe yet shal best power shall perceaue good wyl diligence indeuoure mother dreade womannishe feare shalbe let yf bee naye womannish frowardnesse duke buckingham dare take soule yt wel knoweth yt nedeth suche thyng feare either sonne selfe manne wyll warre womenne would god menne kynne wer womenne bee sone rest none kynne lesse loued bee kynne owne euell deseruing put case nether loued kinne yet cause hate kinges noble brother whose grace oure selues kynne whose honoure yf desyred oure dyshonoure asmuche regarde tooke wealthe owne wyll coulde bee lothe suffer hym absente kyng v yf wytte woulde god good wyll hath frowarde wytte thynketh selfe wiser yt whose feithful myndes nothing doubteth verely beleueth know legeth woulde bee sorye harme owne selfe yet woulde haue hym frome yf abyde thinke bee content bothe child bee came frome thence bee suche place maye bee theyr honoure nowe yf refuse deliueraunce hym folowe wisdome theim whose wisdome knoweth whose approbate fidelitee trusteth easye perceaue frowardnesse letteth feare goo suppose feareth maye let feare owne shadowe feareth deliuer hym oughte feare leaue hym handes yf caste suche fonde doubtes feare hurte wyll feare shall fette thence wyll soone thynke yf menne sette whiche god forbydde greate mischief sanctuarye wyll lytel lette theim whiche sanctuary good menne thinketh myghte withoute synne somewhat lesse regarde dooe nowe yf doubte leaste might bee fetched licklye sende hym oute realme verely looke none doubte nowe sore mindeth mind let therof might hap bring purpose passe great mastery doo letting alone yt world would say sorte wyse councelers aboute king let brother bee cast away vnder nose therfore ensure feithfully minde wyll rather maugre stomacke fetche hym awaye leaue hym tyll feare fonde frowarde feare conuey hym awaye yet wyll breake sanctuarye verely sithe priueledge place yt sorte haue long contynued woulde go breake yt yf nowe begynne would shoulde make theim yet wyl saye nay deede pitie men chauce sea theyr euil debters haue brought pouertee shoulde haue place refuge kepe theyr body dauger theyr cruel credytoures yf fortune croune come question hath done thys time whyle eatch parte taketh traytoures thyncke necessarye haue place refuge theues murtherers whereof place full whyche neuer falle theyr crafte fall therunto yt pytee euer sanctuarye shoulde saue theim especyall wylfull murtherers god commaundeth taken aulter putte death wyse case nede sayntuaryes apointed god olde law yf necessite owne defence mysfortune dryued hym yt deed pardon serueth hym whyche ether grau ted course kynge pytee compassyon geueth nowe looke howe fewe sanctuary necessyte mysfortune compelled together see syde sorte bee commonlye therin suche wylfull vnthryftines hathe broughte naughte rable theues murtherers malycyous heynous traytours bee two place specyallye one elbowe cytee bowel dare wel vowe yf waye good wyth hurte commeth theim ye shall fynde much better lese haue thys say although abused nowe bee longe haue bene feare euer wylbe men feard set theyr handes medement though god saynt peter patron vngratious lyuing vnthryftes riot ronne debte vpon boldnes place yea rytch men ronne thyther poore men goodes buylde spende byd theyr creditours go whystel men wyues ronne thether theyr husbades plate say dare abide theyr husbandes beting theues bring thether stolle goodes lyue thereon deuise newe robbery nightly stele robbe reue kyl men come agayne place though place gaue sauegard harme yt thei haue done licece also myschiefe howbeit much great abusion yf wyse woulde set theyr handes thereunto myghte bee mended great thankes god breche priuiledge conclusion sythe long go wote pope prynce piteous polityke hath graunted men sence relygious feare haue broken yt let v take payne let stande goddes name hys force ferforth reason wyl whyche ferfourth maye serue let v fetchynge forth thys noble manne hys honoure welth place whyche nether nether sanctuary priueledged sanctuarye euer serueth defend bodye man standeth daungers abrode great hurt lawful hurt agaynst vnlawful hurtes harmes pope ner kynge entended priueledge anye one place wherin lawful one man another wrong man vnlaufully take hurte lybertye kynge lawe verye nature biddeth euery place maketh regard euery man euery place sanctuarye wher man lawful meanes parel nedeth tuycion specyall priueledge ground al sanctuary necessitee thys noble prince farre whose loue kyng nature kynred proueth whose innocentie al world hys tender youth affyrmeth sactuary necessary ner none ca haue men com sactuary com baptim require godfather must aske self yt must haue reason sith hath cause haue whose consyence hys faut maketh hauened require wyl hath yoder babe discretio require yf nede wer dare say wold right angry wt theim yt kepe ther wold thik wtout scruple consciece wtout brech priueledge sowhat homly wt yt ther sactuary ded yt yf one go sactuary wt another ma goodes shold ye king leuig body liberty satisfye party goodes eue win ye sactuary nether kyng pope geue anye place priueledge shal discharge man debtes beynge hable pay dyuerse clergie pset whether thei saied pleasure thei thought agreed plainly yt lawe god ye churche yt goodes sanctuary manne bee delyuered paymet debtes stollen goodes owner onely lybertie reserued hym gette lyuyng labour handes verely duke thynke ye saie truth mannes wife take sanctuary list ronne hir husband would thinke ca alledge none cause maye laufully without dyspleasure dooen sainct peter take hir oute sainct peter churche arme bodye maye bee taken oute sanctuary saieth abyde chylde take sanctuary feareth goo schoole master must lette hym alone symple example yet lesse reason oure case though bee chyldyshe feare yet least feare herein feare verely haue heard sanctuary menne neuer harde sanctuary chyldren ther fore conclusio mynde whoso euer maye deserue haue nede thei thinke suretye let theim kepe bee sactuary manne hath nother discresion desire ner malice deserue whose life ner lybertie laufull processe stande ieoperdie taketh one oute sanctuarye dooe hym good saye plainlye breaketh sanctuarye duke dooen temporall mene wholy mooste parte spirituall mene also thynke hurte earthely mente towarde baby condiscended effecte delyuered bee fetched howbeit thei thought best aduoydyng maner rumoure cardynall first assaye gette hym good therupon counsaill came starre chamber westmynster cardinall leauyng protectour lordes sterre chaumber departed sanctuarie quene accompaignied wt certain lordes yt respecte honour personnes many perceaue arrande onely one mane mynde protectoure entended matter trust one manne alone el finally determined kepe hym compaignie paraduenture secrete instruccio incontinet maugre take hym leaue respyte conueigh hym quene lordes come together presence cardynall shewed vnto thought lord protectour whole caunsaill yt hir kepyng yt kynges brother place highly souded onely yt grudge people obloquy also unportable greefe displeasure yt kyng royall maiestie whose grace synguler co forte haue naturall brother compaignie bothes dishonoures hirs also suffre hym sanctuarye though one brother stoode daungier perell shewed ferther whole counsaill sent hym requyre delyuerye hym might bee brought yt kyng presence libertie oute yt place whiche meune reconed prisone bee demeaned accordyng estate degree doyng bothe dooe greate good realme pleasure cousaill profite self succoure frendes destresse ouer yt whiche wist well speciallye tendered onelye greate conforte honoure kyng also younge duke hym self whose bothe greate wealthe bee together aswell many greater cause also bothe dysporte recreacyon whiche thynges lordes estemed sleight though semed light well pode ryng yt youthe without recreacion playe canot endure ner estraunger conuenie cie bothe estate metely yt poinct theim either theim theother lorde quene saie naye conueniente yt gentlemanne requyre compaignie kyng brother good faith thynketh greate commodite theim bothe yet bee custodie mother tendre age consydered elder theim bothe especiall younger whiche besydes infancye also nedeth good lookyng hath awhyle sore deseased syckenesse newlye rather lytle amended well recouered dare putte persone earthely trust wt kepyng self onely consyderyng phisicians saie also fynde double yt perell resylynacion yt first syckenesse whiche desease nature beyng sore laboured forweried weaked waxeth lesse hable bear oute newe surfett albeit might bee fouden would happely dooe best vnto hym yet none yt ether knoweth better howe ordre hym yt log haue kepte hym tendrely like cherishe hym owne mother yt bare hym mane denieth good madame cardinall yt grace folke moost necessarie aboute chyldre would yt cousaill bee content also glad might stand wt pleasure suche place might stade wt honour apoinct self tarie thynke thei coueniet duke yorke yt kyng honorably lybertie coforte theim bothe sanctuary mane bothe dishonoure obloquy sith alwaie greate necessite haue yt childe mother occacio sometyme maye bee suche bee expediet kepe hym el whiche well apereth yt suche tyme yt moost derest soonne prince nowe kyng honour good ordre countre kepe houshold wale farre kepyng grace well cotent therwt self well content quene pet case like theone helth theother nowe sicke whiche case meruell greatly lord protectour desierous haue hym kepyng childe sickenesse miscaried nature yet might rone slaunder suspicion fraude thei call thyng sore childes honoure also abideth place honoures suffre hym abide wher manne doubteth shalbe best kepte whiche yet entend come foorth ieopard selfe fredes whiche would god rather suertie ieoperdie wt theim madame ye lord hawarde knowe thyng thei bee ieopardie naye verely thei bee prisone neither thei nowe bee trowe greate maruell though feare leaste yt haue letted put theim duraunce wt coloure let litle procure distrucion without cause cardinall made countenaunce lord haward harpe vpon yt stryng saied quene yt nothyng doubted lordes kynne whiche remeyned vnder rest vpon matter ramined dooe well ynough toward noble persone neither could bee maner ieopardie wherby truste yt quene yt guyltlesse though thei guyltie yt enemy better beloued thei whe thei hate theim sake nere kyng howe ferre bee thei would helpe god sede grace thei hurt therfore yet purpose departe hence gentlemanne soonne minde shall wher till se se mene gredy whthout substanciall cause haue hym whiche maketh muche afrayd scrupulous delyuer hym truly madame cardynall afrayde ye bee delyuer hym menne feareth suffre kepe hym leaste youre causelesse feare mighte cause farther conueye hym many thynke haue pryuiledge whiche haue neyther wyll aske yet malyce offence nede therfore recon priuiledge broken although fetche hym sanctuarye whiche yf fynallye refuse delyuer hym thynke verely ye councel wil enfraunchese hym muche drede hathe lorde vncle tedre loue beareth hym least grace sende hym awaye ah quene hath tendre zele hym feareth nothyng least escape hym thynketh would sende hym hence whiche neyther plight sende oute place coulde recone hym sure bee sure sanctuarye whereof neuer tyraunte yet deuelyshe durste attempte breake priuiledge truste god nowe stronge wythstande aduersaries euer soonne deserue sanctuarye saye therfore cannot haue forsothe lorde protectoure hath sente goodly glose whiche place may defend may saue innocent ieopardye hath nede thereof woulde god troweth protectoure praye god maye proue protectour rather destroyer whereunto peynted processe draweth honourable duke byde confortable theim bothe brother kyng lacketh playe feloe yea bee sure praye god sende hym better playefelowes hym maketh hyghe matter vpon suche tryfleynge pretexte though coulde none bee founde playe kynge yf brother whiche hathe lu playe syckenesse muste come oute sanctuarye oute sauegarde playe hym though prynces young coulde playe without peres chyldre coulde playe without theyr kynred whome parte agree muche woorsse straungiers chyld saye cannot require priuiledge tolde protectoure aske hym shall hym aske shall ye wyll howebeit straunge matter suppose coulde aske thynke woulde aske ymagene woulde aske go oute yf saye shall note aske priuiledge selfe saye agaynst wyll taketh hym breaketh sanctuarye serueth thys lyberty personne onlye goodes maye frome hence take horsse frome yf stale hym owe nothynge foloweth maye take chylde also ward farre learned councell sheweth hath nothyng dyssente holden knyghtes seruage socage lawe maketh garden maye manne lawfully suppose take warde frome oute thys place wythoute breche sanctuarye yf pryuyledge coulde serue hym aske hym selfe yet sythe lawe commytteth custodye hym maye requyre hym excepte lawe geue infaunte garden onelye hys gooddes dyschargynge hym cure sauekepynge bodye whiche onely bothe goodes landes serue wherfore entende kepe hym sithe mannes lawe serueth garden kepe infaunte lawe nature wylleth mother kepe yt chyld goddes lawe priuiledgeth sanctuarye sanctuarye pryuyledgeth soonne sythe feare putte hym protectoures handes hathe brother already whiche yf bothe fayled inheritoure croune heyre male sayth cause feare man hath dooe examen yet feare law feareth whiche learned menne tell forbyddeth euery manne custody theim whose death maye enheryte lesse lande kyngdome saye whosoeuer bee breaketh holy sanctuary praye god sende hym shortelye nede sanctuary maye come woulde mortall enemie taken sanctuary cardynal perceaued quene euer yt lenger farther also beganne kyndle chafe spake sore bytynge woordes agaynst protectoure suche neyther beleued also lothe sayd finall conclusion would dispute matter contente delyuer duke hym lordes present durste laye owne bodye soule bothe pledge onlye suretie also hys estate surely knewe suspected cause might dooe knewe saide would geue hym resolute aunswere contrarye would therewith departe incontinent shifte woulde wyth busynesse afterwarde neuer entended moue matter whiche thought also saue selfe lacked eyther wytte truthe wytte dull nothyng coulde perceaue protectoure entended yf procure soonne bee delyuered handes whome shoulde perceaue towardes chyld euell wyll entended myghte thynke councell bothe euel aduysed lytle fydelyte theyr prince quene wordes stoode great studye forasmuche sawe lord cardynall redyer departe remanaut protectoure hym selfe redye hande verelye thought coulde kepe hym shoulde bee incontynente taken thence conueye hym elles neyther tyme serue place determyned personnes appoynted conueygh hym thyng vnreadye message came sodenly nothyng lesse lookyng haue hym sanctuarye whiche knewe nowe menne bee set place coulde bee conueyghed oute vntaken partely thought myghte fortune feare bee false well wist ether nede lesse botelesse wherfore yf nedes go hym demed best deliuer hym specially yt cardinalles faith nothing doubted lordes whome sawe feared least might deceaued well assured yt woulde bee corrupted thoughte woulde make theim warely looke hym circum spectly see surety yf owne handes betooke hym theim truste laste tooke young duke hande saied vnto lordes lorde lordes nether vnwise mistruste youre wittes suspicyous mistruste truthes thing purpose make proofe yf either bothe lacked might turne greate sorowe realme muche harme greate reproche lo gentilman whome doubte could kepe salfe would whatsoeuer manne saye doubte also bee abrode deedly enemy vnto bloodde yf wiste laye theyr owne body woulde lette oute haue also experience desyre kingdome knoweth kynred brother hath bene brother bane may nephewes bee sure vncle eache child others defence whyle bee sunder eache liues lyeth others body kepe one salfe bothe bee sure nothing bothe perylous bothe bee one place wise marchaunt neuer auentureth good de one shyp notwithstanding deliuer hym brother hym kepe handes whome shall aske theim bothe god worlde feithfull bee wot well knowe wyse power strength list kepe hym lacke helpe selues nede lacke helpe case yf cannot elles may leaue hym onely one thing besech trust father putte euer truste put nowe farre thincke feare muche ye bee well ware feare lytle therwith saied yt childe fare well myne owne swete soonne god sende good kepyng let kysse gooe god knoweth whe shall kisse together againe therwith kyssed hym blessed hym tourned backe wepte gooing waye leauyng poore innocent chylde wepyng faste mother cardinall lordes receaued younge duke brought hym starre chaumbre yt protectoure tooke hym armes kyssed hym wordes nowe welcome lorde hert saied yt likelihode euen inwardly thought therupon forthwith brought king brother bishoppes palaice powles thence thorowe citee honourably towre oute whiche daye neuer came abrode whenne protectoure bothe chyldren possessyon yee sure place beganne thryste see ende enterprise auoyde suspicion caused lordes whiche knewe bee feythfull kyng assemble baynardes castell comen ordre coronacyon whyle complyces affinitee erosbyes place contriued contrary make protectours kyng whiche counsel adhibite fewe secrete beganne maner muttering amongest people though thing longe bee well though wyste feared wherfore suche great thinges mennes hertes secrete instyncte nature misgeueth theim yt southwinde somtime swelleth hym selfe tempeste one manne happely perceauing fylled many men suspicyon thoughe shewed fewe menne knewe howbeit dealing selfe made muche matter thoughe counsayle close lytle lytle folke drewe towre kyng drewe cro bye place protectoure resorte kyng maner desolate made suyte vnto theim doyng theim theyr frendes secetely warned myghte happely tourne theim good bee muche attendaunte kyng withoute protectoures apoyntmente whiche remoued dyuerse kynges olde seruauntes fro hym set newe theyr rome aboute hym thus many thinges comming together partly chaunce partely purpose caused length comon people onely whiche wauer wt winde wise menne also lordes marke matter muse therupon much lorde stanley whiche afterward erle derby wisely mistrusted saied yt lorde hastinges muche misiyked two seueral couselles talke one matter yt one place lytle wot wherof talke place well lorde hastynges lyfe neuer doubte whyle one man whiche neuer thence neither bee thing mynded shoulde sounde amisse towarde shoulde bee mine eares well oute mouthes ment catesby whiche nere secret councell whome familyerly vsed moost weightye matter putting manne speciall trust hym sith wiste well manne hym muche beholdyng catesbye whiche manne well learned lawes lande speciall fauoure lorde hastynges good authorytee muche rule bare countrees leicestre northampton yt lorde hastinges power laye surely greate pitie either trueth lesse wit dissimulacyon onely kepte myschiefe vp whome yf lorde hastinges put special trust yt lord stanley wt diuers lordes departed coutrees broken al ye daunce many euel signes yt sawe construed al best surely thought coulde harme towarde hym counsayle entended catesbye truth protectour duke buckyngham made good sembleaunce vnto lorde hastynges kepte hym muche theyre compaignie vndoubtedlie protectour loued hym well lothe haue loste hym sauynge feare least hys lyfe shoulde haue quayled theyr purpose whyche cause moued catesby proue wyth wordes caste oute farre whether coulde thyncke possible wynne lorde hastynges theyr part catesby whether assayed hym assayed hym reported vnto hym founde fast heard speake terrible wordes durst farther breake truth lorde hastinges truste shewed vnto catesby mystrust began haue matter therfor fearyng least theyr mocyons myght wt lorde hastynges haue mynished credence wherunto al matter leaned procured protectour hastly ryd hym muche rather trusted hys death obtayne much yt rule whyche lorde hastynges bare hys cou tree onelye desyre whereof thynge enduced hym procurer one speciallest contriuers al thys treason wherupon lorde protectoure caused counsayle set towre frydaye xiii daye iune much commonyng honourable solempnytee coronation whyche tyme appoynted aproched nere pageau te making day nyght westminster vytayle kylled afterwarde cast awaye lordes thus sittyng commoning matter protectoure came emong ix clocke salutynge theim curteously excusynge hym selfe bene frome theim longe saiynge merely bene sseper yt daye lytle talkynge wyth theym sayd bishop ely lorde haue good strawberies garden holborne requyre let v haue messe theim gladly lorde would better thyng redy youre pleasure wyth sente seruaunte al haste dysh strawberyes protectoure set lordes faste commonynge thereupon prayed theim spare hym lytle departed came agayn betwene x xi clocke cha ber al chaunged sowre angry countenauce knyttynge browes frownynge frettynge gnawynge hys lyppes set downe hys place lordes dysmayed sore marueyled thys maner sodayne chaunge thynge hym ayle sytten whyle thus beganne woorthy haue compasse ymagyne dystruccyon beynge neare bloodde kynge protectoure hys royal realme whyche questyon lordes sat sore astonned musynge muche thys questyon shoulde ment whych euery man knewe hymselfe clere lord hastynges familiaritee betwene thoughte myght boldest wyth hym answered sayd worthye bee punyshed heyneous traytours euer affyrmed yonder sorceces brother wyfe wyth meanynge quene wordes manie lordes sore abashed whyche fauoured lorde hastynges better contente hys mynde moued anye loued better albeit hys hearte grudged afore made councel matter well takynge kynred theyr puttynge deathe whyche hys assente deuised behedded pomfrete thys selfe daye whyche ware ye deuysed hym selfe shoulde daye behedded london sayde protectoure wyse ye sorceresse hys counsayle shore wyfe wyth affynitee haue theyr sorcerye wychcrafte thys wasted bodye therewyth plucked vp hys doublet cleane hys elbowe hys lyfte arme shewed weryshe wythered arme small neuer thereupon euery mannes mynd mysgaue theim well perceauynge thys matter quarell well wyste quene boothe wyse goo aboute anye suche foly yf woulde yet woulde al folke make shore wyfe leaste councel womenne hated concubin kyng husband loued also manne knewe hys arme euer syth day hys byrth neuerthelesse lorde hastynges whyche death kyng edward kept shore wyfe somewhat doted kynges lyfe sauynge sayd forbare reuerence towarde hys kynge elles certayne kynd fydelitee towarde hys frende yet nowe heart somwhat grudged haue loued hyghly accused knewe wel vntrulye therefore aunswered sayde certaynlye lord yf haue doone worthie heynous ponyshemente protectoure thou seruest wene wyth yf wyth tell haue doone wyll make good thy bodye traytoure therewith greate anger clapped fyste boorde great rappe whych token geuen one cryed treason withoute chamber therewyth doore claped came rushing men harneyes many chamber coulde holde anone yt protectoure sayd lorde hastynges arrest traytoure lord yea traitour protectour one let flye lord sta ley whyche shroncke stroake fell vnder table elles hed bene cleft teth shortly shrancke yet ranne blood aboute hys eares archebyshoppe yorke doctoure morton byshoppe ely lorde stanleye taken dyuers whyche bestowed dyuers chamber saue lorde hastynges whome protectoure commaunded spede shryue hym apace saint poull dyne till se thy hed booted hym aske heuilie tooke preeste auenture made shorte shrift lenger would bee suffred protectoure made muche haste dyner whiche might goo till murther dooen sauing vngracious othe brought foorth grene beside chapell within towre hed layde dowe logge tymber laye buyldyng ye chapell tyrannously stryken bodye hed enterred wyndesore mayster kyng edward fourth whose soules iesu pardon amen merueleous case either warnynges haue voyded token could voyde next nyght deathe lorde stanley sent hym trusty messenger mydnight hast requiryng hym ryse ryde awaye hym disposed vtterlye lenger abyde fearfull dreame whiche thought bore tuskes rased theim bothe heddes bloodde ranne aboute bothe shoulder asmuche protectour gaue bore cognisaunce ymagened bee dreme made suche fearfull impressio hearte yt throughly determined leger tarye horsso readie lord hastynges would goo hym thei would ryde ferre night thei bee oute daungere next daye good lord lord hastynges messenger leaneth lord thy master muche suche trifle hath suche faith dreames whiche either awne feare fatesieth doo rise yt nightes rest reason dayes thought tell hym plaine witchcraft beleue suche dreames whiche thei token thynges come thynketh yt might likely make theim true goyng caught brought backe frendes fayle flyer bore cause lykely race v tuskes folkes fled falshed wherfore either perell none deede bee rather goyng abydyng nedes fall perell one waye yet leuer menne se mennes falshed thynke either awne faute faynte feble heart therfore goo thy master commende hym praye hym bee mery haue feare assure hym assured yt mane wotteth myne owne hande god sende grace messenger departed certen also rydyng toward towre thesame mornyng whiche behedded horsse accustomed ryde stombled hym twise thrise almost fallyng whiche thyng although happeneth theim daylye myschaunce towarde yet hath olde eiuill token obserued gooyng toward myschief nowe yt foloweth warnyng enuyous scorne thesame mornyng ere vp bed shore wife laye wt hym night came hym sir thomas hawarde soonne lorde hawarde whiche sturryng mornyng earlye courtesie accompaignie hym counsaill forasmuche lorde hastynges readye taried awhile hym hasted hym awaye sir thomas lorde hastynges stayed awhile commonyng preest met towre strete brake lordes tale saiyng hym merely lord praye come wherfore talke long preest haue nede preest yet laughed vpon hym though would saie shall haue nede one sone lytle wist meant night woordes well remembred theim heard theim true lorde hastynges litle mistrusted neuer merier ner thought life suretye dayes whiche thyng often sygne chaunge shall rather lette thyng passe vayne suretye mannes mynde nere deathe vpon towre wharffe nere place hedde sone manne might well cast balle pursyuant awne called hastynges mette wt hym metyng ye place put remembrauce another tyme whiche happened theim mete together ye place whiche tyme ye lord hastynges bee accused kyng edward yt lord ryuers quenes brother somuche yt awhile lasted long highly yt kynges indignacion stode great feare hymself forasmuch nowe met thesame pursyuaunt thesame place ieopardy well passed gaue hym greate pleasure talke hym therof wt talked thesame place matter therfore saied ah hastynges arte thou remembred met heuy herte ye lord remembre well thanked bee god thei gatte good ner harme therby thou woldest saie thou knewest muche dooe whiche fewe knowe yet mo shall shortly meant erle ryuers yt lord richard sir thomas vaughm yt daye bee behedded pomfrette thei deede whiche acte wyst well bee dooen nothyng ware yt axe honge nere owne hed feith manne neuer sorye ner neuer stoode greate daungier life thou mette loe worlde turned nowe nowe stande myne enemy daungier thou mayst happe heare hereafter neuer life meryer neuer greate suertie praye god proue hastynges proue dowtest thou naye naye warraunt maner dyspleased entered towre long lyue haue hearde lord god blyndenesse mortall nature mooste feared moost suretie reconed hym self moost surest loste life yt within ii houres thus ended honorable manne good knight gentle great autorite wt price liuyng somewhat dissolute plain open enemie sure secrete frende easye beguyle good herte courage foresawe perelles louyng manne passyng welbeloued verye faythfull trustie ynough trustyng much destruccion maye perceaue nowe flewe fame lordes death thorough cytie farther like wynde euery mannes eare protectoure immediatly dynner entendynge set coloure vpon matter sent hast many substanciall menne cytie towre commynge hym selfe wyth duke buckyngham stoode harnessed olde euell fauoured bryganders suche manne woulde wene would haue vouchesalued haue putte backes excepte sodeyne necessitee constreigned theim lorde protectoure shewed theim lorde hastynges conspyracye hadde contryued haue sodenly destroyed hym duke buckyngham thesame daye councell entended farther yet wel knowen whiche treason neuer knowledge ten clocke thesame fornoone whiche sodeyne feare draue theim put suche harnesse came nexte theyr hades defence god holpe theim mischiefe turned vpon theim would haue done thus required theim reporte euerye manne aunswered fayre thoughe manne mystrusted matter whiche truthe manne beleued yet farther appeasyng people myndes sent immedyatlye dynner heralde armes proclamacion citee london whiche proclamed kynges name lord hastynges dyuerse treyterous purpose cospired thesame daye haue slain protectoure duke buckyngham sittyng counsaill haue take vpon theim rule kyng realme pleasure therby pill spoyle thei list vncomtrolled muche matter deuised title thing wote wel wylbe loth take vpon whose wisdome wel perceueth ye labour study mynd body yt shal come ther wt hi whosoeuer shal occupy ye rome dare say wyl yf take warrate yt roome childes office yt greate wise man wel perceaued whe sayd regno cuius rex puer est wo realme whose king chylde wherefore much cause haue thank god yt noble personage righteously etitled therto sad age therto great wisdome ioyned wt gret experiece albeit wylbe loth take vpon hi yet shal peticio ye behalfe ye graciously encline ye worshipful cytezins cite beyng chefe cite realme ioyne wt v noble sayd request owne weale doubte yt ye wyll yet neuerthelesse pray wherby ye shall great profite realme beside chosinge good kinge yt shalbe selfe special commodite maiesty shal euer bear much tender fauour much shal perceaue prone beneuolentlye mynded toward eleccion wherin dere frendes mynd haue require playnelye shewe v whe ye duke said loked yt people hoped yt maire framed flatering pposicion made haue cryed kig richard king richard styl mute one word answered wher wt duke meruelously abashed takyng mayre nere hym preuy matter sayde vnto theim softelye meaneth people styll sir mayre percase perceaue wel ye shal amed yf wyl helpe therwith somewhat lowder rehersed matter ordre wordes well ordinately neuerthelesse euydently plain voyce gesture countenaunce comely conuenient euery man muche marueiled yt heard hym thought thei neuer hearde liues euell tale well tolde wer wonder ye eache loked speake fyrst one worde aunswered people stode styll midnight much rounyng emong theim might seme commen beste mayre sawe parteners ye councel drewe duke said yt people bene accustomed ther bee spoken recorder whyche mouth citee happly hym wyl aunswer recorder called thomas fize william sad man honest whiche newly come offyce neuer spoken ye people loth matter begyn notwithstanding therunto commaunded mayre made rehersall comons duke twyse purposed hys self recorder tempered hys tale shewed euery thyng duke wordes parte owne chauge made people whych alwaye one stoode thei bene amased whereupon duke rouned mayre said marueleous obstynate scylence therwith turned people wt woordes deare frendes come moue thyng whiche paraduenture greatly neded lordes realme commos party might haue sufficed sauyng suche loue beare muche set would gladly dooe oute thyng whiche bee parteners weale honoure whiche v semeth se waye wherfore require geue v auswer one whether ye bee mynded noble realme bee haue noble prince nowe protectoure bee kyng woordes people beganne whisper emong theim selfes secretlye voyce nether lowde base like swarme bee till last nether ende halle bushement duke seruauntes one nashfeelde belongyng protectoure prentice laddes thrusted halle emongest preace began sodenly mennes backes crye kyng rychard kyng rychard threwe vp cappes token ioye thei stoode caste heddes maruelyng therat nothyng thei saied duke mayre sawe maner thei wisely turned purpose saied goodly crye ioifull euery manne one voyce mane saiyng naye wherfore frendes duke sith perceaue whole myndes haue noble manne kyng wherof shall make grace effectuall report yt doubte yt shall redounde great wealth comodite therfore requier yt morowe ye go v wt noble grace make humble peticio request hym maner reme bred therwith lordes came downe ye copaignie dissolued departed parte sad glad sembleaunce ye verye merie theim yt came duke hable dissemble sorowe faine euen backe turne face wall doloure heartes brast oute e morowe mayre aldremen chief commoner ye citee best maner appareled asseblyng theim together paules resorted baynardes castel ye tectour laye whiche place also accordyng ye apointement repaired ye duke buckynghm dyuerse noble wt hym besydes many knightes getlemen therupon yt duke sent woord ye lord protectoure ye beyng great honourable copaignie moue great matter grace wherupon protectoure made great difficultie come downe theim excepte knewe part errad though doubted partly mistrusted commyng suche noumbre hym sodenly wtout warning knowledge whether thei came good harme ye duke shewed ye mayre thei might therby se howe litle protectoure looked matter thei set yt messenger suche louyng message ther wt humblie besought hym vouchesalue yt thei might resorte presence purpose entet thei would none persone disclose last came oute chaubre yet downe theim galary ouer theim wt bishop euery thei beneth might se hym speake hym though would yet come nere theim till wist thei meant therupo duke buckynghm first made huble peticio ye behalfe theim yt grace would pardone theim licence theim purpose vnto grace thetent comyng wtout displeasure wtout whiche done obteined thei durst bee bold moue hym yt matter whiche albeit thei meant asmuche honoure grace wealth al ye realme beside yet thei sure howe grace would take thei would wise offende ye protectour verie gentle hym self also loged sore apparautly knowe thei meat gaue leaue purpose hym liked trustyng ye good mind yt bare theim none theim thing would entend hymward wherwt thought bee greued whe ye duke leaue pardo speake wexed bold shewe hym entent purpose wt ye cause mouyng theim therto ye haue hearde finally beseche grace ye would like accustomed goodnes e zeale vnto ye realme nowe wt yie pite behold ye long cotinued distresse decaie yesame set gracious redresse amedemet therof takyng vpo hym ye croune gouernaunce ye realme accordyng right title laufully disce ded vnto hym ye laude god profite surete ye lad vnto grace much ye honour lesse pain neuer prince reigned vpon people glad liue vnder obeysaunce people realme vnder protectoure hearde preposicion looked strangely thereat made aunswer albeit knewe partely thynges theim alledged true yet suche entiere loue bare kyng edward child muche regarded honoure realmes aboute croune one whiche neuer desyrous could fynde hearte poincte incline desyre nacions ye truthe well knowe paraduenture thought owne ambicious mynde deuice depose prince take hym self ye croune whiche infamye would wise haue honoure steyned croune whiche neuer perchaunce perceaued muche laboure pain pleasure hym would vse would worthy haue notwithstandyg perdoned theim mocion thei made hym also thaked theim ye loue hartie fauoure thei bare hym praiyng theim sake beare ye prince vnder whome would bee contente liue laboure cousaill ferre like kyng vse would dooe vttermost deuoyre sette ye realme good estate whiche readye tyme protectourship lauded bee god well begonne ye malice suche occasion contrarie newe entended bee nowe partely good policie partely goddes specyall prouydence mannes prouysion repressed put vnder vpon aunswer geuen duke buckyngham protectoures licence lytle rounded aswell noble menne hym mayre recorder londo vpon like perdon desyred opteyned shewed alowde vnto protectour fynall conclusion realme apoynted kyng edwardes lyne shoulde lenger reygne vpon theim bothe farre gone nowe suretie retreate thought weale vnyuersall take waye although yet begon wherfore woulde like grace take croune vpon hym would humbly beseche hym thervnto woulde geue theim resolute aunswer contrarye whiche would bee lothe muste seke fayle fynde noble man would woordes muche moued protectoure whiche euery manne small intelligece maye wyt would neuer haue enclyned thereto sawe none waye muste take el bothe go sayde lordes commos sith perceaue well realme set whereof sory wyll suffre wyse kyng edwardes lyne gouerne theim whome manne earthly gouerne agaynste owne wylles also perceaue manne whome croune iuste tytle apperteyne selfe right heire lawfully begotten body moste dread dere father rychard late duke yorke title ioyned eleccion noble commos realme whiche tytles possible take moste effectuall content agree fauourably enclyne peticion request accordyng take vpon v royall estate prehemynence kyngdome two noble realmes englande fraunce one fro daye forwarde v oure heyres rule gouerne defende goddes grace good helpe get agayne subdewe establyshe euer due obedience vnto realme englande thaduauncement wherof neuer e god lenger lyue entende procure set foorth greate crye showte criyng kyng richard lordes went vp kyng ye daye called people departed talkyng dyuersly matter euery manne fantasie gaue hym muche thei merueled maner dealyng matter bothe partes made straunge thoughe neuer one parte communed parte therof whe wyst man dul heard theim perceaued well ynoughe matter made betwene theim howbeit excused agayne saiyng thyng muste bee done good ordre men must sometyme ye maner sake acknowe thei third rychard thirde name vsurped croune england ope ly tooke vpo hym kyng xix daye iune yere lord thousand foure hundreth lxxxiii xxv yere lewes xi beyng frenche kyng greate solempnitee rode hys owne beganne wyth moost pyteous wycked meane lamentable murther innocente nephewes yonge kynge hys tender brother whose death fortune hath neuerthelesse farre come questyon remayned long doubte whether dayes destroyed yt parkin warbek many folkes malyce mo folkes folye long space abusynge worlde aswell wt prnceis wt poore people reputed taken younger two also thynges couertly demeaned one thynge prete ted another mente nothynge playne openly proued yet common custome close couert dealyng euer inwardly suspect many well countrefet iewelles make true mistrusted howbeit concernyng opinion menne suche meanes thynketh heard true kyng rychard coranacion takynge howe maner two sone king edward destroyed waye gloucestre visyte newe honoure toune whiche bare name olde deuysed roade fulfyll tirrell deuised thei murthered beddes bloode shed thexecucio wherof apoincted myles forest one foure kepte theim feloe fleshe bred murther tyme ioyned one ihon dighton awne horskeper bygge broade square strong knaue beyng remoued theim myles forest ihon dighton aboute mydnight child beyng beddes came chaumbre murtherynge kynge edward chyldren sodenly lapped theim vp emongest clothes bewrapped theim entangled theim kepyng downe force fetherbed pyllowes heard vnto mouthes yt within awhile thei smored styfled theim brethes faylyng thei gaue vp god innocent soules ye ioyes heauen leauyng tourmetoures bodyes dedde bed whiche ye wretch perceaued first yt strugglyng ye panges dea long liyng still throughly dedde thei laied bodyes vpon ye bed fetched iames tirrell se theim whiche sawe theim perfightly ded caused murtherers burie theim stayre foote metely depe grounde vnder greate heape stone rode iames tirrell great hast kyng rychard shewed hym maner ye murther gaue hym greate thankes mene saye made hym knight alowed buriall vyle corner saiyng yt would haue theim buryed better place thei kynges soonnes lo honourable courage kyng would recompence detestable murther solempne obsequy wherupo preest sir robert brakenburyes tooke theim vp buried theim suche place secretly occasion death whiche verie shortlye whiche onely knewe truthe could neuer yet bee well perfighly knowen saie kyng rychard caused yt preest take theim vp close theim lead put theim coffine full hole hoked ye endes ii hokes yron caste place called ye blacke depes ye thamis mouth yt thei shuld neuer rise vp bee seen ye truth vnknowe reason ye said preste dyed shortly disclosed neuer persone ye would vtter truthe sir iames tirrell towre treason committed kyng hery seuenth bothe dighton examined together poynte bothe thei confessed murther bee dooen thesame maner haue hearde whether ye body remoued thei bothe affirmed thei neuer knewe thus haue learned theim yt muche knewe litle cause lye wer ii noble prince innocet tedre childre borne ye moste royall blood brought vp great welth likely loge liue reigne rule yt realme treyterous tirany taken depriued estate shortly shut vp prison priuely slain murderd ye cruell ambicion vnnaturall vncle dispiteous tourmetours whiche thynges euery part well podered god gaue worlde neuer notable exsample either vnsurety stadeth worldes weale mischief worketh ye proud entreprise high hearte finally wretched ende ensueth suche dispiteous crueltie first begynne wt ye ministres mile forest martines le graud peace meale miserablye rotted awaye ihon dighto liued caleys long lesse disdeined hated poynted dyed great misery sir iames tirrell behedded towre hill treason kyng richard hymself slain ye feelde hacked hewed enemy handes haried horsbacke naked beyng ded heare dispite torne tugged like curre dogge mischeif yt toke wt lesse thre yeres mischief yt thre monethes comperable yet ye meane tyme spet much trouble pein outward much feare dread anguish wt haue heard credible person suche secret wt chauberers yt abhominable dede dooe neuer quiet minde neuer thought hymself sure wet abrode bodie preuely feinted eyen wherled hand euer dagger buckynghm many gentleman hym ye shall next yere occasio duke kyng fell oute dyuerse folke dyuerse wyse pretended duke haue hearde assone duke gloucester death kyng edward come yorke solempne funerall
